In my translation, I have attempted to maintain this tone. The key phrases from the English sentence are "see" and "the whole thing take place," which translate into German as "sehen" and "der gesamte Vorgang stattfinden." I've used "Sie werden" (future tense of "siehe"n, meaning "to see") to convey a sense of anticipation. The word "gesamten" means "entire" or "whole," and "Vorgang" refers to "process" or "procedure." I've also maintained the passive voice found in the original sentence by using "stattfinden," which implies that the action is happening independently of the observer.
